L0005: ## Overview
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0006: This repository implements a reproducible data engineering workflow for NBA player salary modeling. The system ingests tabular player data, applies standardized preprocessing transformations, constructs derived features, validates schema and data quality assumptions, and generates experiment artifacts for downstream modeling and benchmarking.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0007: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0008: The project addresses a common challenge in machine learning systems: obtaining consistent, comparable results across runs and across deployment constraints. In practical settings, preprocessing behavior can drift when input distributions shift or when hardware limits require changes in execution mode. This repository emphasizes deterministic processing, configuration-driven experimentation, and constraint-aware execution so that model development and evaluation remain traceable and reproducible.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0009: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.

L0049: ## Memory Hierarchy and Cache Effects
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0050: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0051: The project does not capture PMU counters directly, but practical signals include:
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0052: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0053: - Increased `encode_scale_s` with larger chunks may indicate cache pressure during one-hot encoding.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0054: - Rising end-to-end latency with stable throughput can indicate memory copy overhead.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0055: - Divergence between bandwidth estimate and throughput can indicate storage or serialization bottlenecks.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0056: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.

        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.

        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.

L0061: - enable `--spill-to-disk`
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0062: - reduce `--chunk-size`
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0063: - keep `--max-memory-mb` realistic for resident process limits
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0064: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0065: For CPU-constrained systems:
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0066: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0067: - lower `--max-compute-units`
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0068: - use smaller `--batch-size`
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0069: - keep `--n-jobs 1` to avoid contention
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0070: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0071: ## Assumptions
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.

        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.

FILE: docs/streaming_workflow.md

L0001: # Streaming Workflow and Runtime Analysis
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0002: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0003: ## End-to-End Workflow
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0004: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0005: 1. Load source data and create a deterministic fingerprint.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0006: 2. Derive initial chunk and batch sizes from configured memory and compute limits.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0007: 3. Preprocess each chunk and build streaming-safe features.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0008: 4. Validate chunk outputs and collect telemetry snapshots.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0009: 5. If memory limits are exceeded, reduce chunk size and retry (bounded).
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0010: 6. Update online learning state with `partial_fit` per accepted chunk.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0011: 7. Write chunk-level logs and aggregate benchmark artifacts.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0012: 8. Emit a final report with quality checks, performance summaries, and drift metrics.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0013: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0014: ## Runtime Behavior Under Constraints
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0015: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0016: - **Adaptive chunk resizing** lowers OOM risk at the cost of additional orchestration latency.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0017: - **Compute-aware scaling** reduces chunk/batch sizes when compute budget is capped.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0018: - **Spill-to-disk mode** preserves progress in low-memory environments with extra I/O latency.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0019: - **Telemetry integration** captures CPU load, RSS memory, system memory pressure, and optional RAPL energy.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0020: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0021: ## Layer-Wise Latency and Memory Decomposition
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0022: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0023: The pipeline is organized into four major operators per chunk:
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0024: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0025: 1. Clean and normalize records.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0026: 2. Build and update engineered features.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0027: 3. Drop high-correlation features and encode/scale inputs.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0028: 4. Run model update/evaluation.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0029: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0030: Interpretation guidance:
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0031: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0032: - If preprocessing dominates latency, investigate parsing and categorical handling.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0033: - If feature encoding dominates memory, inspect category cardinality.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0034: - If model update latency grows with chunk size, retune chunk/batch parameters.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0035: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0036: ## Bandwidth and Utilization Notes
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0037: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0038: - Input bandwidth is driven by CSV read rate and storage throughput.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0039: - Memory bandwidth pressure increases during one-hot encoding and concatenation.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0040: - CPU utilization can spike during bootstrap/permutation statistics in benchmarks.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0041: - Throughput should be evaluated jointly with peak RSS to avoid unstable operating points.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0042: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0043: ## Precision and Quantization Trade-Offs
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0044: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0045: Current implementation uses floating-point operations in pandas/numpy/scikit-learn defaults.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0046: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0047: - Lower-precision representations can reduce memory footprint.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0048: - Precision reduction may change model quality and drift estimates.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0049: - Quantization is not enabled by default and should be validated per deployment target.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0050: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0051: ## Assumptions
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0052: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0053: - Input schema is stable across chunks.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0054: - Benchmark runs are executed with a fixed seed.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0055: - Artifact paths are writable for all report outputs.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0056: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0057: ## Limitations
        ↳ Comment line documenting intent or usage context.
L0058: 
        ↳ Blank line used for readability and logical separation.
L0059: - Operator-level metrics are derived from stage and chunk timing, not kernel profilers.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0060: - Energy estimates are approximate when hardware counters are unavailable.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
L0061: - Cache/memory hierarchy effects are inferred from trends rather than hardware PMU counters.
        ↳ Executable/source line contributing to program logic or data definition.
